add_namespace = fate_of_AFG
country_event = {
	id = fate_of_AFG.1
	title = fate_of_AFG.1.t
	desc = fate_of_AFG.1.d
	#picture = 
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = fate_of_AFG.1.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {	country_exists = AFG	}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = AFG
					remove_government_ideas = yes
					every_state = {	limit = {	is_core_of = AFG	}	remove_core_of = PREV	}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	AFG_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
						add_core_of = PREV
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = AFG_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = PREV	}
				}
			}
			else = {
				AFG = {
					remove_government_ideas = yes
					every_state = {	limit = {	is_core_of = AFG	}	remove_core_of = PREV	}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	AFG_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						AFG = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
						add_core_of = AFG
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = AFG_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = AFG	}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = fate_of_GRL.1.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {	country_exists = GRL	}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = GRL
					remove_government_ideas = yes
					every_state = {	limit = {	is_core_of = GRL	}	remove_core_of = PREV	}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	GRL_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
						add_core_of = PREV
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = GRL_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = PREV	}
				}
			}
			else = {
				GRL = {
					remove_government_ideas = yes
					every_state = {	limit = {	is_core_of = GRL	}	remove_core_of = PREV	}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	GRL_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						GRL = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
						add_core_of = GRL
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = GRL_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = GRL	}
				}

		}

	desc = fate_of_VAT.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = fate_of_VAT.1.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {	country_exists = VAT	}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = VAT
					remove_government_ideas = yes
					every_state = {	limit = {	is_core_of = VAT	}	remove_core_of = PREV	}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	VAT_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
						add_core_of = PREV
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = VAT_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = PREV	}
				}
			}
			else = {
				VAT = {
					remove_government_ideas = yes
					every_state = {	limit = {	is_core_of = VAT	}	remove_core_of = PREV	}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	VAT_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						VAT = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
						add_core_of = VAT
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = VAT_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = VAT	}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = fate_of_COM.1
	title = fate_of_COM.1.t
	desc = fate_of_COM.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = fate_of_COM.1.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {	country_exists = COM	}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = COM
					remove_government_ideas = yes
					every_state = {	limit = {	is_core_of = COM	}	remove_core_of = PREV	}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	COM_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
						add_core_of = PREV
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = COM_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = PREV	}
				}
			}
			else = {
				COM = {
					remove_government_ideas = yes
					every_state = {	limit = {	is_core_of = COM	}	remove_core_of = PREV	}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	COM_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						COM = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
						add_core_of = COM
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = COM_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = COM	}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

						VIR = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
						add_core_of = VIR
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = VIR_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = VIR	}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

add_namespace = fate_of_WIW
country_event = {
	id = fate_of_WIW.1
	title = fate_of_WIW.1.t
	desc = fate_of_WIW.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = fate_of_WIW.1.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {	country_exists = WIW	}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = WIW
					remove_government_ideas = yes
					every_state = {	limit = {	is_core_of = WIW	}	remove_core_of = PREV	}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	WIW_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
						add_core_of = PREV
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = WIW_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = PREV	}
				}
			}
			else = {
				WIW = {
					remove_government_ideas = yes
					every_state = {	limit = {	is_core_of = WIW	}	remove_core_of = PREV	}
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	WIW_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						WIW = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
						add_core_of = WIW
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = WIW_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = WIW	}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
